01:37:47","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","title":"This is what it's like to order from Floracracy, a flower delivery service that makes custom arrangements you help design.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/floracracy-flower-delivery-review","description":"<p class=\"financial-disclaimer\"><i>If you buy through our links, we may earn money from affiliate partners. <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.insider-inc.com/commerce-on-insider-inc/\">Learn more.</a></i></p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dafed70954f0019195974?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 lead\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li aria-level=\"1\"><strong><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Floracracy</a> is a relatively new flower delivery service and offers custom arrangements you design yourself.</strong></li>\n<li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>It makes some of the most beautiful arrangements I&#39;ve ever seen, and the flowers lasted for weeks.</strong></li>\n<li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>It took home the title of &#34;best for custom arrangements&#34; in our <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-flower-delivery-service\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">guide to the best flower delivery services</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><bi-shortcode id=\"table-of-contents-sticky\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"h2\">Table of Contents: Masthead Sticky</bi-shortcode><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"small\" data-pid=\"5fe2695d19a2461f3024d82d\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Personalized Flower Arrangements (small)</bi-shortcode><p>There are times when it&#39;s nice to brighten someone&#39;s day with a bouquet, and occasions in life that are truly worth marking with a stunning arrangement. <a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Floracracy</a>, which just launched in October 2020, caters to life&#39;s most meaningful moments by crafting custom floral arrangements that feel unique, personal, and extra special.</p><p>I recently had the opportunity to try Floracracy as part of testing for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-flower-delivery-service\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">our guide to the best flower delivery services</a>. I&#39;m not exaggerating when I say that it made the most stunning arrangement I&#39;ve ever received from a flower delivery service. It could have easily taken the top spot in our testing for the beauty and longevity of the arrangements, but because the design process is more involved and trends pricier, we ended up naming it the &#34;best for custom arrangements.&#34;</p><p>That said, this is now the first company I think of when I contemplate sending blooms to someone, and I already have a long list of people I can&#39;t wait to gift a stunning Floracracy bouquet to. Here&#39;s what I love about the service</p><h2>How it works</h2><p>The process starts with <a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Floracracy&#39;s</a> design tool, which walks you through designing your custom arrangement with a quiz. You choose the occasion, your relationship to the recipient, the mood you most want to convey, and the style of flowers you want (whimsical, garden, Old World, etc). Since I was sending flowers to myself, I chose the &#34;strictly decor&#34; occasion, which then prompted me to fill in where in my house I expected to display the flowers; I chose &#34;coffee table,&#34; and selected the &#34;garden&#34; style. </p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dd9fd30004b0019b266c3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 screenshot\" height=\"600\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A screenshot of the design tool, which lets you customize the shape, color palette, and specific flowers in your arrangement.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider via Floracracy website</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a>The tool then makes recommendations for a certain shape arrangement that fits your needs, or you can choose from other available styles that fit your criteria. Once you choose a shape and size, you can customize every detail of the arrangement - from the color palette down the individual types of flowers used. I loved this feature, since it let me choose peachy colors that I knew would work well with the warm hues in my living room decor, and I could choose flowers I was sure would be safe to have around my cat. When you hover over each flower in the arrangement, the tool shows you the flower&#39;s meaning and origin, so you can better craft a piece that sets the mood you wish to convey.</p><p>I ultimately chose the Juliette shape in the garden style, and customized it with ferns and three different types of roses. I chose delivery later that week, though next-day delivery is available. If you&#39;re sending the arrangement to someone, you&#39;ll be given the option to craft a letter or have the company write a letter based on information you provide.</p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606db21470954f0019195979?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 screenshot arrangement\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A screenshot of the bouquet I designed and ordered.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider via Floracracy website</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>The process took me about 20 minutes, mostly because I wanted to browse through all the available options, which meant sometimes retaking the quiz. It&#39;s only been a few months since <a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Floracracy</a> launched, but I would love to see better navigation in the design tool; it was hard to toggle back if I changed my mind about shape, style, or color. That said, I love being able to preview my custom bouquet, and the curation provided by the quiz format felt really unique.</p><p>According to the website, Floracracy will also be launching a &#34;design it for me&#34; option soon, for those who don&#39;t want to go through the design process themselves.</p><h2>Delivery options</h2><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Price range:</strong> $155 to $350</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Delivery area:</strong> Lower 48 states</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Same-day delivery:</strong> No</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Next-day delivery:</strong> Yes</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Shipping:</strong> Included</li></ul></aside><p>One of the great things about Floracracy is that shipping is included with the price of your arrangement, which lowers the overall cost (shipping for flowers can get quite expensive). While there isn&#39;t currently an option for same-day delivery, you can choose next-day delivery for the lower 48 states. This is the option my coworker went with, while I opted for delivery a few days out. Both our arrangements arrived on time and in excellent condition.</p><h2>Review of Floracracy </h2><p>Since the arrangement I chose has a large, distinct shape, I was curious to see how it would ship and arrive. A few days later I got my answer when a large, almost 3-foot tall box arrived on my doorstep. </p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606db68d30004b0019b265fb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 delivery box\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>There was a lot of packaging, and unboxing the arrangement required the help of my partner, but unboxing still felt special and exciting. Inside the shipping box, I was greeted by a gift box festooned with ribbon and adorned with my personalized letter and a small pair of gold-accented mini shears. Lifting the box lid uncovered the most lush, gorgeous floral arrangement I had ever seen: a whimsical array of garden roses in varying warm tones, each vibrant and perky and adorned by wild-looking ferns and foliage. </p><p>Every arrangement also comes with a coordinating vase, a handbound book for pressing petals, and an illustrated card with each of the flowers and their meaning. The total package felt like a stunning and special gift. </p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dc38830004b0019b2663a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 flower arrangement 1\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>My arrangement I ordered. I chose the “Juliette” shape in the “garden” style and customized the flower colors and types.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>The included materials on flower care were the most robust I&#39;ve seen from any service, but the instructions also include information on how to dry and preserve the flowers or petals. I love that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fshareasale.com%2Fr.cfm%3Fb%3D999%26u%3D1088116%26m%3D100985%26urllink%3Dfloracracy.com%252F%26afftrack%3Dxid%3Afr1617722855276hef&source=5a6f97de59d4326f038b46d2&sessionid=16177228512789lu2brzc&afftrack=1617722851617azo6tp2ne&xid=fr1617722855276hef1617722855276hef\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Floracracy</a> acknowledges that fresh flowers are a fleeting gift, and still offers suggestions to enjoy your arrangement through all the stages of its life. The care instructions also noted that if you donate your empty vase to a women&#39;s shelter and let Floracracy know, the company will send them flowers, which I thought was a lovely touch. </p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606db73e70954f0019195990?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 accessories\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Each arrangement comes with a vase, small shears, a personalized letter, a print of the flowers and their meanings, and a book for pressing petals.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>I was incredibly impressed by the lifespan of the fresh flowers. Almost three weeks after receiving it, the arrangement still had many fresh blooms and foliage among the drying flowers, and it still looked artful and healthy enough to display. A colleague who ordered and received a smaller Floracracy arrangement reports her blooms have lasted just as long.</p><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606db80270954f0019195998?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 2 weeks later\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>My arrangement about two weeks later. The blooms drooped a bit and I had to weed out a few dying buds, but for the most part it was still very lively.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Lauren Savoie/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><h2>Cons to consider</h2><p>While very fairly priced for what you&#39;re receiving, one downside is that Floracracy doesn&#39;t offer many options at more affordable price points. Expect to spend at least $155 on this service, with more impressive options costing up to $300. </p><p>It&#39;s also not the ideal choice if you&#39;re just looking to quickly pick out a bouquet and be done with the process - the service requires at least a little of your time and thought to get the most out of it, and the tool can be a bit tricky to navigate if you don&#39;t have your mind made up about what you want. </p><h2>The bottom line</h2><p><a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&u=1088116&m=100985&urllink=floracracy.com%2Fcracy.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606db85b70954f001919599b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"floracracy flower delivery service review 2021 alternate arrangement\" height=\"3024\" width=\"4032\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A smaller Floracracy arrangement ordered by my coworker.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Connie Chen/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p><p>That said, the result is one of the most personalized and special bouquets your loved one will likely ever have been gifted. For me, receiving and displaying the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fshareasale.com%2Fr.cfm%3Fb%3D999%26u%3D1088116%26m%3D100985%26urllink%3Dfloracracy.com%252F%26afftrack%3Dxid%3Afr1617722855276bhb&source=5a6f97de59d4326f038b46d2&sessionid=1617722851278xttrtsb0&afftrack=1617722851617ahgv5ix9f&xid=fr1617722855276bhb1617722855276bhb\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Floracracy</a> bouquet was one of the highlights of my winter, and I already have plans to use this service for upcoming holidays and celebration</p><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Completely customizable arrangements, online tool helps you choose the right arrangement, beautiful presentation and packaging, thoughtful extras like a petal pressing book and mini shears, letter writing service</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Online tool can be a bit tricky to navigate, lots of packaging (though most is compostable or recyclable), few budget options</p><bi-shortcode The PS5 sets a new standard for gaming hardware, and Sony says it plans to continue supporting the PS4 for years to come. The PS5 also supports nearly every PS4 game, so gamers can transfer their library to the new console whenever it&#39;s time to upgrade.</p><p>Below, we&#39;ve collected the best deals on PlayStation consoles, games, and accessories. Third party headsets designed for PlayStation 4 will also work for PS5, including wireless models.</p><p>The PlayStation VR is the top-selling VR headset, thanks in part to the 100 million people who already own the required PS4. The headset connects directly to the console and can be used to play standard games in 2D as well as immersive VR titles like \"<a href=\"https://shop-links.co/1737110699911509321\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Firewall: Zero Hour</a>.\"</p><p>The PlayStation Move Motion controller has been around since the days of the PS3 and works in tandem with the PlayStation VR to track arm and hand movements. The subscription also offers special discounts in the PlayStation Network store, and subscribers get free games each month that remain available as long as the PlayStation Plus subscription is active.</p><p>PlayStation 5 owners who subscribe to PlayStation Plus receive a collection of more than 20 free games. Think Netflix, but for PlayStation games. The service includes games for PS2, PS3, and PS4. As an added bonus, console owners can download the full version of PS4 games from PlayStation Now to play offline. The service is comparable to Microsoft's Xbox Game Pass.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"medium\" data-pid=\"5dadef034af90945ce252be5\" data-purchase-option=\"\">12-Month Subscription (medium)</bi-shortcode><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-cardtype=\"medium\" data-pid=\"5defcf9dfd9db20c41050bbe\" data-purchase-option=\"\">3-month Membership (medium)</bi-shortcode>\n\tBest PlayStation console deals\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f9806fb4743a3001216bd40?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PlayStation 5 PS5 PlayStation 4 PS4 Comparison\" height=\"1196\" width=\"1595\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The PlayStation 4 and PlayStation 5, side by side.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kevin Webb / Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Sony released the&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/sony-ps5-playstation-5-review\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">PlayStation 5</a> in November 2020, but don't expect to find any deals on the next-gen console. src=\"https://i.insider.com/601b238aee136f00183aa314?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Alphabet &#38; Google CEO Sundar Pichai\" height=\"1642\" width=\"2190\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Google CEO Sundar Pichai speaks during Google I/O 2016\n<p class=\"copyright\">Justin Sullivan/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Google I/O is coming back for 2021, and will be held remotely May 18-20, 2021, according to a puzzle invite sent on Wednesday.</li>\n<li>The conference was canceled entirely last year because of the pandemic.</li>\n<li>I/O is Google&#39;s biggest annual event, where it showcases upcoming software updates and, occasionally, new hardware.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Google will return to its annual I/O developer conference this year after skipping last year&#39;s event due to the pandemic. It will be free and held in an online-only format, according to an invite sent out early on Wednesday.</p><p>The conference will be held May 18-20, according to the invite, which was distributed as a puzzle and cracked by <a href=\"https://9to5google.com/2021/04/07/google-i-o-2021-announced/\">9to5Google</a>.</p><p>Google skipped 2020&#39;s I/O conference due to the coronavirus pandemic. The event was scheduled to run May 12-14, but in early March the company announced it would move to an online-only format. It later <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-cancels-io-conference-coronavirus-concerns-2020-3\">canceled</a> it entirely.</p><p>Calls for product groups to nominate products and speakers for 2021&#39;s event went out in January, according to one current employee. Another said that Google had been pre-recording videos for the event in recent weeks. Both asked to remain anonymous because they were not authorized to speak to the press.</p><p>I/O is Google&#39;s biggest annual event and is typically held at the Shoreline Amphitheatre, near the company&#39;s headquarters in Mountain View, California. Its 2019 conference drew more than 7,000 attendees. A Google spokesperson declined to comment on this year&#39;s conference.</p><p>Google uses I/O to showcase advances in its software and AI, including upcoming changes to the Android smartphone operating system. </p><p>Although Google typically holds a separate event for hardware later in the year, it has launched new devices at I/O in the past, including new additions to its Pixel smartphone line.</p><p><a href=\"https://9to5google.com/2021/04/06/google-email-inadvertently-leaks-green-pixel-buds-a/\">Some recent reports</a> suggest the company has some imminent announcements for its smartphone lines - maybe I/O is where we&#39;ll hear about them.</p><p><em>Are you a current or former Google employee with a tip? You can contact this reporter securely using the encrypted messaging apps Signal and Telegram (+1-628-228-1836) or via encrypted email (hslangley@protonmail.com). Reach out using a nonwork device.</em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Langley)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/601b238aee136f00183aa314?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn64@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-29-243_2e1835dc0a19b715.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn8@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-29-454_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=aCYDZiDELmU:TNDUfH4ADa4:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn84@2020_2/2021/04/07/17-38-28-412_08f7955a6736b213.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=aCYDZiDELmU:TNDUfH4ADa4:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn15@2020_5/2021/04/07/17-38-26-403_1105d2aed2e386c4.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn15@2020_4/2021/04/07/17-38-27-264_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=aCYDZiDELmU:TNDUfH4ADa4:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn67@2020_5/2021/04/07/17-38-30-021_cf3873ecb0bc452b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/aCYDZiDELmU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn99@2020_4/2021/04/07/17-38-27-966_b683e6a16b5623da.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617817067340},{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","title":"Biden's campaign made 2 promises on canceling student debt. He hasn't done either.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/student-debt-cancelation-biden-campaign-promise-public-college-hbcu-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dbc1830004b0019b26615?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Joe Biden\" height=\"1332\" width=\"1777\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>President Joe Biden.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Mandel Ngan/AFP via Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Biden made campaign promises to cancel $10,000 in student debt per person and forgive debt for students from HBCUs and public colleges.</li>\n<li>As president, he has not yet followed through on either promise.</li>\n<li>The DOE has already canceled debt for defrauded borrowers and borrowers with disabilities.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>So far, President Joe Biden&#39;s Department of Education has acted to address the <a href=\"https://educationdata.org/student-loan-debt-statistics\">$1.7 trillion student debt crisis</a> in the country by, among other things, canceling debt for some borrowers defrauded by for-profit schools and for borrowers with disabilities.</p><p>On his first day in office, Biden&#39;s first action addressing student debt was to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-extend-pause-federal-student-loan-payments-on-first-day-2021-1\">extend the pause</a> on federal student loan payments through September. Since then, Education Secretary Miguel Cardona has taken <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-biden-has-done-to-tackle-student-debt-crisis-2021-3\">three distinct steps</a> to confront student debt: he canceled debt for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-education-secretary-student-loan-debt-cancels-department-defrauded-borrowers-2021-3\">about 72,000 borrowers</a> defrauded by for-profit schools, he canceled debt for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-education-department-cancels-student-debt-borrowers-disabilities-paperwork-cardona-2021-3\">over 41,000 borrowers</a> with disabilities, and most recently, he expanded the scope of the payment pause to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-education-department-expands-pause-student-loan-debt-payments-private-2021-3\">1.14 million borrowers</a> with private loans. </p><p>But as president, Biden has yet to follow through on two campaign promises he made to voters on cancelling student debt. The more than 81 million people who voted for him also voted for two promised actions on student-debt relief that haven&#39;t been enacted yet, if they ever will be.</p><p>Regarding further actions Biden might take on student debt cancelation, a DOE spokesperson told Insider that the department &#34;is working in partnership with colleagues at the Department of Justice and the White House to review options with respect to debt cancellation.&#34;</p><p>Here&#39;s what Biden said on the campaign trail about how he&#39;d tackle the student-debt crisis:</p><h1>Cancel $10,000 in student debt per person </h1><p>During his campaign, Biden promised to immediately cancel $10,000 in student debt per person. In a <a href=\"https://www.rev.com/blog/transcripts/joe-biden-speech-on-economic-recovery-plan-transcript-november-16\">speech</a> on November 16, Biden said that student loans are holding borrowers up, and forgiving $10,000 in student debt &#34;should be done immediately.&#34;</p><p>Biden&#39;s campaign <a href=\"https://joebiden.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/UNITY-TASK-FORCE-RECOMMENDATIONS.pdf\">website</a> said the president would work with Democrats to &#34;authorize up to $10,000 in student debt relief per borrower&#34; as part of COVID-19 relief, but the $1.9 trillion stimulus package he <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stimulus-biden-signs-trillion-covid-relief-package-checks-direct-payments-2021-3\">signed</a> in March didn&#39;t include that. He also said he would support legislation brought to him to cancel $10,000 in student debt, but Sen. Elizabeth Warren of Massachusetts said in a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/warren-schumer-biden-cancel-student-debt-executive-order-keep-pressure-2021-3\">press call</a> last month that doing so is lengthy and expensive, and while she has legislation to do it, there&#39;s no reason Biden can&#39;t use executive action to provide the immediate relief he had promised.</p><p>Warren campaigned on a larger number, advocating the cancelation of $50,000 of debt per person, and she and Senate Majority Leader Chuck Schumer have been urging Biden to act on that. At a CNN town hall in February, Biden said he <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-wont-cancel-student-debt-heres-why-go-big-economy-2021-2\">doesn&#39;t have the executive authority</a> to cancel up to $50,000 in student debt per person, but said he is prepared to cancel $10,000.</p><p>&#34;My point is: I understand the impact of debt, and it can be debilitating,&#34; Biden said at the town hall. &#34;I am prepared to write off the $10,000 debt but not $50 [thousand], because I don&#39;t think I have the authority to do it.&#34;</p><p>Biden has since asked the <a href=\"https://www.whitehouse.gov/briefing-room/press-briefings/2021/02/17/press-briefing-by-press-secretary-jen-psaki-and-deputy-national-security-advisor-for-cyber-and-emerging-technology-anne-neuberger-february-17-2021/\">Justice Department</a> and the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-wants-to-cancel-student-loan-debt-ron-klain-says-2021-4\">Education Department</a> to review his authority to use executive action to cancel student debt, indicating he may act on this promise. He may go even further, as White House Press Secretary said in early April that the $50,000 cancelation figure <a href=\"https://www.google.com/url?sa=t&rct=j&q=&esrc=s&source=newssearch&cd=&cad=rja&uact=8&ved=0ahUKEwimprG8r-zvAhWhTd8KHcioBKwQxfQBCHIwCA&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.businessinsider.com%2Fbiden-student-debt-50k-executive-order-rule-out-psaki-2021-4&usg=AOvVaw1-bD7mMgY1mYPGDGiO-p6f1-4&#38;usg=AOvVaw1-bD7mMgY1mYPGDGiO-p6f\">hasn&#39;t been ruled out</a>. But nearly three months into his presidency, he hasn&#39;t acted on this yet.</p><h1>Cancel debt for undergraduates from public colleges and HBCUs</h1><p>Another plan Biden had to address student debt during his campaign was to <a href=\"https://joebiden.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/UNITY-TASK-FORCE-RECOMMENDATIONS.pdf\">forgive</a> all undergraduate tuition-related federal student loan debt for borrowers from public colleges and universities earning up to $125,000 per year, and it would also apply to private Historically Black Colleges and Universities (HBCUs) and minority-serving institutions.</p><p>Forgiving debt for borrowers who attended HBCUs would help address the racial wealth gap in the student debt crisis. Insider previously reported that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-americas-student-debt-crisis-impacts-black-students-2019-7\">86.6% of Black students</a> take out federal student loans, compared to just 59.9% of white students. </p><p>This plan was modeled after Sen. Bernie Sanders of Vermont and Rep. Pramila Jayapal of Washington&#39;s <a href=\"https://www.sanders.senate.gov/press-releases/college-for-all-act-introduced/\">College for All Act</a>, introduced in 2017, which would make public colleges and universities tuition-free and reduces student debt.</p><p>&#34;If we are to succeed in a highly competitive global economy and have the best-educated workforce in the world, public colleges and universities must become tuition-free for working families and we must substantially reduce student debt,&#34; Sanders said in a statement.</p><p>The Education Department has not yet released any information on this plan.</p><p>The department did not provide Insider with a timeline for when further cancellation measures will occur. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the 01:37:47","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","title":"Under-30s should no longer be offered the AstraZeneca vaccine, UK regulators say, citing rare blood clots","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/under-30s-shouldnt-take-astrazeneca-vaccine-uk-regulator-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606da5fb70954f0019195953?format=jpeg\" alt=\"AstraZeneca\" height=\"1259\" width=\"1678\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty/WPA Pool</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>People under the age of 30 should not be offered the AstraZeneca vaccine, UK officials said.</li>\n<li>It follows reports of very rare - and potentially fatal - blood clots in people who got the shot.</li>\n<li>Officials said the decision was taken as young people face more risk of the clots, and less risk from COVID-19.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The AstraZeneca coronavirus vaccine should not be given to people under the age of 30, UK officials said Wednesday.</p><p>The UK&#39;s Joint Committee on Vaccines and Immunisation (JCVI) <a href=\"https://www.gov.uk/government/publications/use-of-the-astrazeneca-covid-19-vaccine-jcvi-statement/jcvi-statement-on-use-of-the-astrazeneca-covid-19-vaccine-7-april-2021\">recommended offering under-30s another vaccine instead</a>, though it said those who have already had one shot should get their second.</p><p>In a statement, the group said that under-30s should be &#34;offered an alternative COVID-19 vaccine, if available.&#34;</p><p>Most people under 30 have not yet been offered vaccines in the UK, which concentrated on older demographics first.</p><p>The reason for the change is a small number of blood clots in people given the vaccine. Officials at the briefing described them as a &#34;suspected&#34; side-effect of the shot, and said that they are very rare.</p><p>They argued that the benefits of the vaccine - preventing people being hospitalized and killed by COVID-19 - still far outweigh the risks.</p><p>Around the same time as the UK announcement, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astrazeneca-vaccine-side-effects-blood-clots-very-rare-ema-2021-4\">regulators in the EU said that they believe the clots should be formally listed as a side-effect of the vaccine</a>, though they also argued that the benefits of using it outweigh the risks.</p><p>At the briefing Wednesday, Jonathan Van-Tam, the Deputy Chief Medical Officer for England, described the change as a &#34;course correction.&#34;</p><p>Dr June Raine, Chief Executive of Medicines and Healthcare products Regulatory Agency (MHRA) said of the blood clots that &#34;the risk of this rare suspected side effect remains extremely small.&#34;</p><p>The logic of restricting the vaccine from use in younger demographics is that they are less at risk of COVID-19, and slightly more at risk from the clots, officials said at the briefing.</p><p>This chart from the MHRA was shown to describe the balance of risks:</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dc78730004b0019b2664c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"chart\" height=\"935\" width=\"1819\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>This chart shows the risk to benefit balance for the AstraZeneca vaccine in different populations, according to the MHRA.\n<p class=\"copyright\">MHRA</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>As of March 31, the MHRA recorded 79 cases of the blood clots following the first dose of the AstraZeneca vaccine (51 women and 28 men age from 18 to 79 years). Of those, 19 died, three of whom were less than 30 years old.</p><p>The 19 deaths were from many millions of people in the UK to be given the AstraZeneca jab. The country has given out more than 20 million doses. More details on the people who got clots was <a href=\"https://www.gov.uk/government/news/uk-regulator-confirms-that-people-should-continue-to-receive-the-covid-19-vaccine-astrazeneca\">published in an MHRA press release</a>.</p><p>Similar reports of blood clots prompted earlier suspensions of the AstraZeneca rollout in many countries, some of which later restricted the use of the shot in younger age groups.</p><p>Countries including, Canada, Germany, France, and Italy have suspended the use of the vaccine <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astrazeneca-covid-19-vaccine-no-evidence-to-stop-use-ema-2021-3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astrazeneca-covid-19-vaccine-no-evidence-to-stop-use-ema-2021-3\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">in younger populations</a> pending the results of the investigation.  </p><p>The shot has not been approved in the US. Dr. Antony Fauci, the White House chief medical advisor the US <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/idUSKBN2BO6XS\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/idUSKBN2BO6XS\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">may end up not needing</a> the AstraZeneca vaccine for its vaccine rollout. </p><p>The AstraZeneca vaccine makes up three-quarters of the vaccine supply in the UK, the <a href=\"https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-9444603/Is-Britains-Covid-vaccine-roll-brink-disaster.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-9444603/Is-Britains-Covid-vaccine-roll-brink-disaster.html\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">Daily Mail reported on Wednesday</a>.</p><p>It also makes up a substantial proportion of vaccination programmes in other countries, including lower income countries depending on the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/africa-astrazeneca-suspension-threatens-to-fuel-vaccine-hesitancy-2021-3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/africa-astrazeneca-suspension-threatens-to-fuel-vaccine-hesitancy-2021-3\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">COVAX scheme</a>.</p><div src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dc54070954f00191959da?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Grab\" height=\"3128\" width=\"6256\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/photos/grab-ride-hailing?agreements=pa:105700&#38;family=editorial&#38;phrase=grab%20ride%20hailing&#38;sort=best#license\" target=\"_blank\">ROSLAN RAHMAN/Getty Images</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The Singaporean rideshare giant Grab is set to merge with the SPAC Altimeter Growth 1, according to a report from The Financial Times.</li>\n<li>The deal values the combined company at $35 billion and will give $2.5 billion in financing to Grab.</li>\n<li>Grab grew revenues 70% year-over-year in 2020 despite COVID-19 headwinds. </li>\n<li aria-level=\"1\"><strong><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingeste=markets&#38;utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&#38;utm_medium=ingest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>The Singapore-based ride-hailing and delivery giant Grab is reportedly set to list in the US via a SPAC merger with Altimeter Growth Corp. 1.</p><p>The deal values the combined entity at $35 billion, according to three unnamed sources from <a href=\"https://www.ft.com/content/73d8b26c-3d61-48ec-8027-25c4cd625488\">The Financial Times</a>,</p><p>Grab will raise $2.5 billion in total financing through a private investment in public equity (PIPE) in the deal, with $1.2 billion coming from Altimeter Growth 1.</p><p>The figures of the proposed merger are still subject to change, the Financial Times report added.</p><p>Grab was founded in 2012 by Anthony Tan and Tan Hooi Ling and has raised some $12 billion thus far on its journey to Southeast Asian rideshare dominance, despite never earning a profit.</p><p>The company has about $5 billion in cash reserves and grew revenues 70% year-over-year in 2020.</p><p>Grab&#39;s backing comes mainly from the Japanese conglomerate SoftBank which <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/r-uber-rival-grab-raising-2-billion-from-softbank-chinas-didi-wsj-2017-7\">invested</a> $2 billion in the Singaporean firm back in 2017 at a roughly $5 billion valuation.</p><p>Grab also operates a fintech subsidiary called <a href=\"https://www.grab.com/sg/grab-financial-group/\">Grab Financial</a> which was started after an $856 million funding round from Japanese investors Mitsubishi UFJ Financial Group and TIS INTEC in February 2020, per TechCrunch.</p><p>Grab Financial then raised more than $300 million in a Series A funding round led by the South Korean firm Hanwha Asset Management in January. The subsidiary&#39;s total revenues grew more than 40% in 2020.</p><p>Grab <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/softbank-backed-ride-hailing-firm-grab-set-to-announce-layoffs-sources-2020-6\">laid off</a> about 5% of its workforce in 2020 as COVID-19 hurt business operations, but the company says it&#39;s ride-hailing business is  &#34;breaking even in all of its operating markets,&#34; per the Financial Times. </p><p>Grab is set to merge with Altimeter Growth Corp. 1, one of two SPACs run by Altimeter Capital and ex-Zillow board member Brad Gerstner. The SPAC raised $450 million after going public on the NASDAQ in 2020.</p><p>If the Grab merger is finalized and approved at its current valuation it will be the biggest SPAC deal in history.</p><div height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 07 Apr 2021 15:28:18 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/606dc54c70954f00191959db?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"5aacd2cfaf733c6a7bda5a92d53e8d79","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn19@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-23-595_822a8b6304b028d0.webp","destWidth":5560,"destHeight":4170,"sourceBytes":524648,"destBytes":524648,"author":"wdaniel@businessinsider.com (Will Daniel)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/606dc54070954f00191959da?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn43@2020_1/2021/04/07/17-38-27-881_d9e8f5502f3ec5af.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn8@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-29-454_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=uFnq7WtpbFs:YnHFGOAJ3Pw:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn79@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-25-072_90ff5f9ba74c6bb2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=uFnq7WtpbFs:YnHFGOAJ3Pw:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn52@2020_6/2021/04/07/17-38-30-003_44ed64a34f532475.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn15@2020_4/2021/04/07/17-38-27-264_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=uFnq7WtpbFs:YnHFGOAJ3Pw:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn63@2020_5/2021/04/07/17-38-26-652_3d7699877fe75c45.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/uFnq7WtpbFs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn24@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-30-390_151d443a367235f5.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617817067357},{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","title":"An F-35 pilot explains how the Air Force's fighter jets have evolved from generation to generation","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/pilot-explains-differences-between-generations-of-us-fighter-jets-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dcf2e70954f0019195a2d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"f-35 heritage flight mustang sabre f-16\" height=\"877\" width=\"1755\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>An F-86 Sabre, top, an F-22 Raptor, middle, and an F-16 Fighting Falcon flying out of Davis-Monthan Air Force Base in Arizona, March 5, 2016.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/airmanmagazine/25358171393/in/album-72157663941160663/\" target=\"_blank\">US Air Force photo by J.M. Eddins Jr.</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A fighter generation is a time period when aircraft are designed and built with similar philosophy and technology.</li>\n<li>There&#39;s no clear-cut distinction between them, but looking back on them allows you to understand how they differ, explains Justin Lee, a US Air Force F-35 pilot.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>I hear the term &#34;fighter generation&#34; a lot these days, such as fourth-gen or fifth-gen. What does that mean?</p><p>It&#39;s a great question. A <a href=\"https://www.sandboxx.us/blog/everything-you-need-to-know-about-fighter-generations/\">fighter generation</a> is a period of time where aircraft were designed and built with similar technology, under a similar philosophy.</p><p>There&#39;s no clear-cut distinction between generations - engineers simply build the best aircraft they can and looking back we can broadly categorize where different aircraft belong.</p><p>Fifth-generation aircraft represent the newest fighter technology. However, to understand what that means and what capabilities these aircraft bring to the table, we need to take a look at the previous generations.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dd05d70954f0019195a34?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Air Force P-80 fighter jet\" height=\"923\" width=\"1263\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A US Air Force P-80, the US&#39;s first operational jet fighter, in flight in 1946 or 1947.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The dawn of the jet age began during WWII with the first operations jet - the German Me-262. The United States, lagging in <a href=\"https://www.sandboxx.us/blog/the-royal-navy-is-testing-jet-pack-assault-teams/\">jet technology</a>, fielded their first combat-capable jet in 1945.</p><p>These and other first-generation aircraft were like their propeller-driven predecessors, except for their engines. They had little to no avionics, and their primary weapon was the gun.</p><p>Because jet engine technology was in its infancy, they had short lifespans and, if not delicately managed, were prone to flameouts - quickly turning them into gliders.</p><p>After the Korean War ended in 1953, second-generation fighters made their debut. One of the lessons learned during the war was that gunning a high-speed aircraft with a manual gunsight was incredibly difficult. Technology had also progressed to the point where missiles could be used to shoot down enemy aircraft.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dcd9770954f0019195a1c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Air Force F-104A\" height=\"1185\" width=\"1800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Two US Air Force F-104A Starfighters around 1960.\n<p class=\"copyright\">National Museum of the US Air Force</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Combined with afterburning engines, this era gave rise to the interceptor: high-speed, high-altitude aircraft, like the F-104 Starfighter, that was designed to intercept Russian bomber formations and launch <a href=\"https://www.sandboxx.us/blog/americas-air-to-air-nuke-would-have-taken-out-entire-bomber-fleets/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">nuclear-tipped air-to-air missiles</a>.</p><p>Third-generation aircraft arrived in the early 1960s. These aircraft placed an emphasis on a multi-role capability.</p><p>Aircraft like the F-4 Phantom could carry a variety of air-to-air and air-to-ground weapons, including the first laser-guided smart-bombs. The gun was de-emphasized and, in some cases, eliminated.</p><p>This, combined with subpar missile reliability, led to a lower-than-expected air-to-air kill ratio during the Vietnam War.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/56ec259c91058425008b74ba?format=jpeg\" alt=\"F 4 phantom camo\" height=\"1611\" width=\"2496\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>F-4 Phantom II fighters in formation during a heritage flight demonstration.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Aircraft_camouflage#/media/File:1997_F-4_Heritage_Flight_over_Florida-edit_1.jpg\" target=\"_blank\">USAF - MSgt Michael Ammons</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Fourth-generation aircraft addressed the missile-reliability issue by reemphasizing the importance of maneuverability and the within-visual-range dogfight.</p><p>Nimble aircraft based on fly-by-wire control systems (instead of traditional cables and pulleys) were developed, which allowed inherently unstable designs like the F-16 Viper to fly.</p><p>Avionics were also substantially improved, along with the pilot-to-aircraft interface. By placing the buttons on the stick and throttle, a pilot could execute thousands of commands without taking their hands off the controls, allowing for quicker reaction times and the ability to change settings under high G-forces.</p><p>Because several fourth-generation aircraft are still flying today, many include a fourth-and-a-half generation designation for aircraft that were upgraded or redesigned after the 1990s.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/604f7d9187891e0019850cc8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Air Force F-15EX fighter jet\" height=\"932\" width=\"2000\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The first F-15EX is delivered to its new home at Eglin Air Force Base in Florida, March 11, 2021.\n<p class=\"copyright\">US Air Force/Tech. Sgt. John McRell</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Due to an exponential increase in computing power over the last 50 years, the fourth-generation aircraft rolling off the factory-line today - like the F-16V and the <a href=\"https://www.sandboxx.us/blog/why-is-america-buying-the-f-15ex-instead-of-more-f-35s/\">F-15EX</a> - are massively improved from their original designs.</p><p>Though they may look similar to their predecessors, their advanced integrated avionics suites allow for an order of magnitude increase in situational awareness.</p><p>Because fifth-generation aircraft were designed from the ground up nearly 30 years after their fourth-generation predecessors took flight, an entire article needs to be devoted to describing the new capabilities these aircraft bring to the fight. Make sure to keep an eye out for part 2!</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">REUTERS/Benoit Tessier</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>\n<p>KKR-backed AppLovin is targeting a $30 billion valuation page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Mobile-gaming company AppLovin is targeting a $30 billion valuation for its US initial public offering, with plans to raise as much as $2.13 billion, <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/applovin-ipo/update-2-mobile-gaming-firm-applovin-aims-for-over-30-bln-valuation-in-u-s-ipo-idUSL4N2M02KC\">Reuters first reported Wednesday</a>.</p><p>AppLovin, backed by private equity firm KKR, is looking to sell 25 million shares between $75 to $85 each. </p><p>The Palo Alto, California-based company applied to list under the Nasdaq ticker symbol &#34;APP.&#34;</p><p>Banks underwriting the deal are led by Morgan Stanley, JP Morgan, KKR, BofA Securities, and Citigroup. </p><p>AppLovin, founded in 2012, is the latest in the long list of mobile gaming firms looking to profit from pandemic-stricken gamers who are stuck at home due to the pandemic. DraftKings, Playtika Holding, and Roblox all recently went public.</p><p>The company has been scaling up. In February, AppLovin <a href=\"https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20210203005880/en/%C2%A0CORRECTING-and-REPLACING-AppLovin-to-Acquire-Mobile-App-Measurement-Market-Leader-Adjust-to-Expand-its-Global-Technology-Platform\">acquired Berlin-based Adjust</a>, a mobile app measurement and marketing company. In May 2020, the company <a href=\"https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20200514005454/en/AppLovin-to-Acquire-Machine-Zone-to-Expand-Leadership-Position-in-Mobile-Gaming\">acquired Machine Zone</a>, best known as the developer of top-grossing mobile games including &#34;Game of War: Fire Age, Mobile Strike,&#34; and &#34;Final Fantasy XV: A New Empire.&#34; Sources valued the deal at about $500 million, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-03-03/kkr-backed-applovin-files-for-nasdaq-listing-after-posting-loss\">according to Bloomberg</a>. </p><p>Last year, AppLovin reported a $126 million net loss, according to Reuters, compared to a net profit of $119 million in 2019.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a>.</strong></li></ul><p>Investing in non-fungible tokens is a &#34;huge risk,&#34; according to the entrepreneur who spent $69 million on an NFT has said. His voice is the latest in a growing number of figures to strike a skeptical tone about the market.</p><p>Vignesh Sundaresan, a crypto investor who cofounded bitcoin ATM company BitAccess, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-04-06/crypto-whale-behind-69-million-nft-sees-huge-risk-for-traders?sref=Yg3sQEZ2\">told Bloomberg</a> on Tuesday that investing in NFTs is &#34;even crazier than investing in crypto.&#34;</p><p>Sundaresan&#39;s warning came despite the fact that the entrepreneur spent <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/beeple-nft-mike-winkelmann-digital-art-christies-2021-3?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestm=ingest\">$69 million</a> buying an NFT artwork by Beeple called &#34;Everydays: The First 5,000 Days.&#34; It made Beeple the third-most-expensive living artist.</p><p>&#34;I don&#39;t think NFTs will hold the same kind of hype forever around high-value items,&#34; Sundaresan, who is also known as MetaKovan, told Bloomberg. &#34;The market will get divided. There will be very few high-value items and an infinite number of very low-valued items.&#34;</p><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-does-nft-mean-crytpo-non-fungible-tokens-art-explained-2021-2#:~:text=Non%2Dfungible%20tokens%20account%20for,of%20Insider%20for%20more%20stories.?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestm=ingest\">Non-fungible tokens, or NFTs</a>, are a special class of digital assets that cannot be exchanged with one another for equal value, or broken down into smaller bits. They often operate as a type of collectors&#39; item and cannot be duplicated.</p><p>They are the hottest new thing in the crypto world, with superstar artist <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/damien-hirst-nft-non-fungible-token-ethreum-palm-currency-project-2021-3-1030258965\">Damien Hirst</a> and musicians <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/snoop-dogg-lionel-richie-nfts-non-fungible-token-cryptocom-marketplace-2021-3-1030237655?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\">Lionel Richie and Snoop Dogg</a> getting in on the game.</p><p>But there are signs that the initial wave of interest in NFTs may be declining. Data from <a href=\"https://www.theblockcrypto.com/post/100240/did-we-already-see-the-peak-of-the-nft-boom\">The Block</a> showed that weekly NFT trading volumes reached $196 million in late February. But it had tumbled to $34 million by March 28.</p><p>Crypto exchange founder Bobby Lee told Insider that he thought a bubble is forming in some parts of the market.</p><p>He said that the technology itself is sustainable, but added that investors should be cautious about getting into specific classes of NFTs.</p><p>&#34;Likely it can get over-hyped and you could lose money,&#34; he said.</p><p>Antoni Trenchev, co-founder of crypto banking firm Nexo, told Bloomberg TV on Wednesday that he was also concerned about a bubble in NFTs.</p><p>&#34;If there&#39;s anything akin to a bubble within crypto I would argue it&#39;s within the NFT space,&#34; he said. &#34;One has to be cautious this late in the bull cycle with NFTs.&#34;</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a Near record trading volume on its platform as <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/btc-usd\">bitcoin</a> surged to record all-time highs boosted Coinbase&#39;s earnings results.</p><p>&#34;We continue to believe COIN&#39;s product experience and best-in-class compliance and regulatory controls should provide a defensible moat,&#34; the note said, before adding that management at Coinbase is well prepared to protect its business if a bear market in bitcoin materializes. </p><p>&#34;It is no question that Coinbase&#39;s revenue is highly correlated to bitcoin,&#34; Luria said. Bitcoin soared 104% in the first quarter to just under the $60,000 level, <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-rally-stalls-60000-resistance-level-crypto-btc-eth-2021-4-1030281754\">which has consistently served as resistance over the past two months.</a></p><p>DA Davidson derived its $440 price target from a 20x multiple on Coinbase&#39;s expected 2021 revenue. <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/coinbase-valuation-hit-90-billion-private-auction-market-public-march-2021-3-1030162598\">Coinbase last traded at $350 per share</a> in a private auction on the Nasdaq Private Market, affording the company a $90 billion valuation. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a Marjorie Taylor Greene raised $3.2 million in her first three months in Congress.</li>\n<li>The size of her haul is almost unheard of for a first-term congresswoman. </li>\n<li>Greene stirred multiple controversies and was kicked off her committee assignments. </li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>In her first three months in Congress, Rep. Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez, for example, <a href=\"https://www.nydailynews.com/news/politics/ny-ocasio-cortez-new-york-delegation-fundraiser-20190417-aykxjxdd4zffrf42joyd36wjhq-story.html\">brought in $726,000 in her first quarter in office in 2019</a> and <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-election-fundraising-aoc/u-s-representative-ocasio-cortez-raised-1-2-million-in-second-quarter-idUSKCN1UA2KR\">$1.2 million in the second quarter of 2019. </a></p><p>Other high-profile House Democrats and Republicans have similarly boasted big hauls, but Greene&#39;s grassroots fundraising is particularly notable given that her House colleagues, including 11 fellow Republicans, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/republicans-who-voted-strip-marjorie-taylor-greene-of-committee-assignments-2021-2\">voted to remove her from her assignments</a> on the House Committee on Education and Labor and the House Budget Committee. </p><p>The last Republican to be stripped of committee assignments after making controversial comments, former Rep. data-uri=\"25b5b3aa30e5a297556fe7a05fabe861\"> disturbing social media postings</a> from before Greene was elected to Congress in which she suggested that several mass shootings were hoaxes and endorsed other conspiracy theories.</p><p>Several months after the shooting, Greene posted an article to Facebook about former Broward County sheriff&#39;s deputy Scot Peterson getting a shooting.&#34; </p><p>In a separate Facebook post, Greene wrote, &#34;I am told that Nancy Pelosi tells Hillary Clinton several times a month that &#39;we need another school shooting&#39; in order to persuade the public to want strict gun control.&#34;</p><p>In other old social media postings, Greene suggested that top Democrats including House Speaker Nancy Pelosi <a 01:37:47","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:37:47","title":"Vaccine passports are spreading across the world. Here's how they could work in the US","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/vaccine-passports-coronavirus-how-will-they-work-in-us-israel-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606de07e30004b0019b266fe?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport israel 4\" height=\"1240\" width=\"2480\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Attendees show off their &#34;green passes&#34; (proof of being fully vaccinated against COVID-19 coronavirus disease) as they arrive at Bloomfield Stadium in the Israeli Mediterranean coastal city of Tel Aviv on March 5, 2021\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Vaccine passports are set to become a part of daily life across much of the world.</li>\n<li>Restaurants, gyms, sports stadiums, and other venues could require digital documents as proof a person has been vaccinated.</li>\n<li>Israel has already rolled out a vaccine passport scheme and other countries are close behind.</li>\n<li>Here&#39;s how the schemes work.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Vaccine passports are set to become a part of everyday life right across the world as governments race to vaccinate their populations against the coronavirus.</p><p>Countries including Israel, the United Kingdom, and much of Europe have either already rolled out a vaccine passport scheme or are actively working on one.</p><p>While the US government says it <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/do-i-need-proof-of-covid-19-vaccination-to-travel-2021-3\">won&#39;t introduce federally mandated vaccine passports</a>, it does look increasingly likely that many restaurants, gyms, sports stadiums, and other venues will require such a document to prove they have been vaccinated against COVID-19 and they <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/do-i-need-proof-of-covid-19-vaccination-to-travel-2021-3\">may also be required for international travel.</a></p><p>So what might a vaccine passport system look like in the United States? </p><p>One model the US government and businesses could look to is Israel, which has led the world both in terms of vaccinating its population and in introducing a vaccine passport scheme.</p><p>Here&#39;s what their scheme can tell us about how vaccine passport systems might work in the US.</p><h2>How do vaccine passports work?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606ddcdf30004b0019b266d6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"israel vaccine passport\" height=\"850\" width=\"1701\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Israeli Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu, center, holds a &#34;Green Pass,&#34; for citizens vaccinated against COVID-19, as he visits a fitness gym with Austrian Chancellor Sebastian Kurz\n<p class=\"copyright\">Associated Press</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>Israel <a href=\"https://www.insider.com/do-i-need-proof-of-covid-19-vaccination-to-travel-2021-3\">started issuing so-called &#34;green passes&#34; on February 21</a> to people who had received the second dose of a COVID-19 vaccine. Under the scheme, designed to ease the country out of lockdown, Israelis issued their ID or passport number, date of birth, and approval for their health care provider to verify that the person had received their vaccine.</p><p>In return, they were issued with a &#34;green pass.&#34; The <a href=\"https://corona.health.gov.il/en/directives/green-pass-info/\">pass can be displayed on a mobile phone as a QR code or as a printed physical document</a>.</p><h2>Who is eligible for a passport?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606ddf2970954f0019195a95?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport israel 5\" height=\"1358\" width=\"2717\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>Every adult who has been received two doses of a COVID-19 vaccination, or who has recovered from the coronavirus. Children younger than 16 years old who have recovered from the coronavirus can be added to their parent&#39;s passport.<h2>Where does a the pass allow you to enter?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dddcf30004b0019b266e2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport israel .JPG\" height=\"992\" width=\"1984\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>Anyone is allowed to enter a museum or art gallery. Those with a green pass <a href=\"https://corona.health.gov.il/en/directives/green-pass-info/\">can enter venues including</a>:</p><p>- Gyms and studios<br>- Swimming pools<br>- Restaurants and cafes<br>- Hotels<br>- Stadiums and other sporting venues<br>- Theaters<br>- Cinemas</p><h2>What does a vaccine passport mean for travel?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606dde3730004b0019b266e7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport 3.JPG\" height=\"1240\" width=\"2480\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>Israel&#39;s government has been tight-lipped about when it will start to significantly ease current travel restrictions, which prevent citizens from traveling abroad on holiday. However, <a href=\"https://www.google.com/url?sa=t&rct=j&q=&esrc=s&source=web&cd=&cad=rja&uact=8&ved=2ahUKEwi3i7ebwezvAhWng_0HHeMKDZkQFjACegQIAhAD&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.arabnews.com%2Fnode%2F1809061%2Fmiddle-east&usg=AOvVaw08Ah-SuPUl05GfC1ZUtIkXast&#38;usg=AOvVaw08Ah-SuPUl05GfC1ZUtIkX\">it has signed an agreement with Cyprus and Greece, two EU members, to pilot a scheme</a> that allows vaccinated people to travel freely between the three countries, Arab News reported. It will be piloted this summer.</p><h2>Has Israel&#39;s roll-out of vaccine passports gone well?</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606de03130004b0019b266fa?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport 8\" height=\"1240\" width=\"2480\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>&#34;In the shopping mall no one is really checking on [vaccine passports] but in restaurants and bars it&#39;s working,&#34; said Tal Schneider, a political correspondent at The Times of Israel in an interview with <a href=\"https://newseu.cgtn.com/news/2021-04-05/How-is-Israel-s-vaccine-passport-working-and-should-Europe-follow--Zchw9FgZVe/index.html\">CGTN Europe</a>.</p><p>Schneider said the public reaction to passports had been positive, where people felt it had &#34;added&#34; to their freedom.</p><p>&#34;You&#39;ve seen people outdoors everywhere and indoors everywhere,&#34; she said. &#34;It&#39;s made a lot of people feel easy to participate,&#34; she said.</p><h2>Counterfeit vaccine passports could be a problem</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606ddfa770954f0019195a98?format=jpeg\" alt=\"vaccine passport israel 6\" height=\"1240\" width=\"2480\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>There are major privacy issues with Israel&#39;s vaccine passport program, however.<p>The QR codes which the green pass scheme relies on are easily counterfeited and a black market for forged passports has reportedly emerged already on Telegram, the encrypted chat app.</p><p>According <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/rbarzik/posts/3872539906117567\">to Ran Bar-Zik</a>, a cybersecurity expert in Israel, &#34;there are tens of thousands faking&#34; green passes. His comments were <a href=\"https://www.timesofisrael.com/thousands-reportedly-attempt-to-obtain-easily-forged-vaccinated-certificate/\">cited by the Times of Israel</a>.</p><p>Another issue is that the scheme relies on a centralized database, <a href=\"https://www.telegraph.co.uk/technology/2021/03/30/flawed-technologies-behind-vaccine-passports/\">the Telegraph reported</a>. That means everyone&#39;s personal information is kept in one place, creating a potential goldmine for hackers.</p><p>However, a spokesman for Israel&#39;s health ministry said the early versions of Israel&#39;s green passes had been developed quickly and new versions would be more secure.</p><p>&#34;We are looking into implementing a secure barcode that will be internationally accepted,&#34; <a Although an hour away from Vermont's popular ski resorts, this Putney property is in close proximity to orchards, wineries, and hiking trails.&#160;</p><p>Availability is open throughout the rest of the year.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Sleeps:&#160;</strong>4 guests/2 bedrooms</p><p><strong>Rating: </strong>4.96</p></aside>\n\tSleek, cozy cottage in Morristown, $157\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5edaa0431918240e572825c9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Best Airbnbs in Vermont\" height=\"960\" width=\"1280\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Airbnb</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.airbnb.com%2Frooms%2F6010241%3Fsource_impression_id%3Dp3_1615238447_rdKivhxLIwGMpSpe%26guests%3D1%26adults%3D1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Book this home in Vermont on Airbnb starting at $157 per night</a></h2><p>From the outside, this stone and wood cottage seems like a modest country abode. But inside, interiors are modern with a lofted sleep area, midcentury-inspired furniture, recessed lighting, and light wood beams.&#160;</p><p>Up to four guests can enjoy the basic, but advantageous amenities, including a patio with a grill, air conditioning, and an in-home washer-dryer. The Morristown home base is near ample breweries, state parks, cider mills, and biking trails.</p><p>This home has scattered dates in spring and summer and is fully available starting in fall.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Sleeps:&#160;</strong>4 guests/2 bedrooms</p><p><strong>Rating: </strong>4.97</p></aside>\n\tMini house built by sculptors in Pownal, $195\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f6117b857b7da001ee11cf9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Vermont airbnb unique home\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Airbnb</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.airbnb.com%2Frooms%2F35160747%3Fsource_impression_id%3Dp3_1615238468_ETI3SHTP58DeNPG0%26guests%3D1%26adults%3D1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Book this house in Vermont on Airbnb starting at $195 per night</a></h2><p>For those seeking a whimsical, one-of-a-kind stay, Owl Hill House is an organically shaped structure built by a group of sculptors in the early 1980s that was recently renovated by one of its original creators.</p><p>The unconventional look might conjure images of Hobbits, Adobe enclaves, or even the Flintstones, but the interior design is bright and airy with hand-plastered white walls and smooth domed ceilings. Fixtures and furnishings include a dining area, shelves, plush seating, and a sleeping area, which were all custom-made and built into the very design of the home.</p><p>There's also a well-stocked kitchen, fireplace, and outdoor seating that overlooks a tranquil meadow and clearing surrounded by trees on a private Vermont dirt road.</p><p>This home has full availability starting in June.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Sleeps:</strong> 2 guests/1 bedroom</p><p><strong>Rating: </strong>5.0</p></aside>\n\tAlpine A-frame in the woods in Wilmington, $289\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f610e40323fc4001e0d6685?format=jpeg\" alt=\"best vermont airbnbs\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Airbnb</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.airbnb.com%2Frooms%2F42485715%3Fsource_impression_id%3Dp3_1615238625_C4vF3HgHZRZY8Y%252BO%26guests%3D1%26adults%3D1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Book this cabin in Vermont on Airbnb starting at $289 per night</a></h2><p>Inside and out, this alpine A-frame is downright stunning, from the bright blue walls to the enchanting interiors crafted from solid wood, flanked by a wood-burning stove, midcentury modern furniture, and a cozy bedroom with a Nectar Queen-sized mattress and organic linens.&#160;</p><p>Small details also shine, from the lighting that includes both a sleek installation and fairy tale twinkle lights, as well as a record player, farmhouse-inspired kitchen, and creature comforts such as AC, Wi-Fi, and P.F. Candle and Beekman 1802 products.</p><p>The home is also dog friendly (for a small fee) and comes with the use of a fire pit and deck with Weber grill and outdoor dining set for a meal under the stars. A short stroll away is a lovely lake and hikes, skiing, shopping, and state parks are all nearby.</p><p>This popular home has availability starting in June.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Sleeps:&#160;</strong>2 guests/1 bedroom</p><p><strong>Rating: </strong>4.85</p></aside>\n\tFAQ: Traveling to Vermont\n\t\n\t<h2>Where is Vermont?</h2><p>The state of Vermont is located in the Northeast, within the region of states known as <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-airbnbs-new-england\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">New England</a>. It's in between New York and New Hampshire, and is located above Massachusetts, running up to the Canadian border.</p><h2>What is there to do in Vermont?</h2><p>Vermont is an outdoors dream, renowned for its mountainous areas that are great for skiing in winter, hiking in spring and summer, and leaf-peeping in the fall when the lush foliage puts on a spectacular show of changing hues of yellow, burnt orange, and crimson red, drawing visitors from around the world. But it's not all woodsy; impressive lakes add to the ample scenery.</p><p>Come and sample homemade cheese and maple syrup from seasonal stalls at local farmer's markets, sip on craft ciders and brews, and shop in charming stores in small towns. Larger cities like Burlington are home to universities, buzzy dining, and great shopping.</p><h2>How far is Vermont from New York City?</h2><p>Southern Vermont ski areas such as Stratton, Mount Snow, Putney, and Okemo are about a 4-hour drive from New York City. Northern regions such as Stowe or Burlington are closer to 6 hours by car.</p><h2>Where is there to stay in Vermont?</h2><p>If you want to ski in winter but seek a shorter drive from major cities like New York, consider Southern Vermont towns such as Dover, Stratton, Brattleboro, Bennington, Putney, Ludlow, or Killington as your base. You'll find many Airbnb vacation rentals in these areas that cater to skiers and snowboarders. These homes also make great places to stay in warmer weather when many mountains open to hikers.</p><p>For more of a city vibe, you'll want to head north to Burlington, or the capital, Montpelier. For something woodsy and remote, you can pick from pretty much anywhere else.</p><h2>Is it safe to rent an Airbnb in Vermont?</h2><p>The CDC says <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-fully-vaccinated-travelers-can-now-travel-in-the-us-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">fully vaccinated people can safely travel in the US</a>.</p><p>Additionally, experts say&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-airbnbs-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">Airbnb is safe</a>, especially&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/which-is-safer-airbnb-hotels-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">compared to hotels</a>, because they eliminate interactions with others. Airbnb hosts must also follow&#160;<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/airbnb-new-cleaning-protocol\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\">enhanced cleaning g</a>uidelines.</p><p>Of course, there are still risks and we recommend following CDC guidelines, practicing social distancing, double masking, and washing hands frequently.</p>\n\tMore of the best Airbnbs in the Northeast\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ff34d9f6056b60018721c28?format=jpeg\" alt=\"catskills Airbnb\"
